Large Quantities of White Rice Exported to Japan 125

Rice Prices Soar Accordingly

Food Panic Suddenly Arises

According to the Shanghai News Agency, this year's autumn harvest was abundant, and rice prices were low. White rice (commonly known as No. 2 rice) was only worth about seven silver dollars per stone, which was convenient for the common people. Unexpectedly, rice prices have suddenly risen to 8.2 silver dollars recently. The reporter specifically investigated the reasons for the price increase with rice merchants. It is said that Japan produces Indica rice, which the Japanese do not like to eat. Therefore, Japanese rice merchants often purchase white rice from our country to sell in the market. This year, rice prices in our country are low, so Japanese merchants have prepared funds to purchase and transport large quantities of rice, engaging in hoarding. This can both profit from it and promote famine in our country, which is a consistent policy of harming others and benefiting themselves. It is a pity that Shanghai merchants mostly only care about their immediate interests and sell rice to the Japanese, which has caused a sudden panic in the rice market, and rice prices have risen daily. It is heard that rice shops in this city, such as Changfengyi, Xiechangde, Taixiang, and Yusheng, have sold large quantities of No. 2 rice, which were resold to Japanese merchants by brokers and shipped abroad by Japanese ships.

The General Management Office of the Bank of China in the city recently suddenly withdrew the Heihe Office in Heilongjiang and transferred all personnel to the Harbin Branch. General Ma Zhanshan, chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, telegraphed the Management Office, requesting that it immediately withdraw the order, waive the withdrawal, and maintain the status quo. He hoped that the Bank of China, being patriotic, would not lag behind others and would be able to comply. The original telegram was extremely painful and critical. The Daily News Agency reporter recorded the original text from the United Northeast Armies' Shanghai Communications Office yesterday:

To Liu Piguang, Director of the United Northeast Anti-Japanese Armies' Shanghai Communications Office, transfer to the Management Office of the Bank of China in Shanghai, Please acknowledge the letter from the Heihe Office of your bank: "Our office received a telegram from the head office stating that Heihe has been without business for a long time, the customs have also been withdrawn, and there are no more taxes to collect. We are instructed to close the office and transfer all personnel to the Harbin branch to avoid losses. We will comply immediately and prepare to go to Harbin. Please check." We find that your bank's establishment, closing, and mergers of offices and branches are appropriate measures for your bank to coordinate business. We have no need to comment. However, Heihe's office is in a special situation, and it is the only financial institution for anti-Japanese resistance in the Northeast. All transfers of comfort funds and circulation of commercial funds rely on it. This is because most of the merchants along the border are foreigners. Whether they are purchasing goods or sending money home, they rely on remittance to turn things around. Since your bank stopped Heihe's remittance, it has already felt deeply inconvenient. Fortunately, the consolation funds could be used to circulate, and the lifeline of the local area could be maintained. This government, considering that the consolation funds are temporary and dare not hope for them to be long-term, intends to telegraph your office to restore remittance to maintain this anti-Japanese base. Suddenly, we received a new order to withdraw, cutting off this lifeline. The banks in our Chinese territory, which are being relied upon for circulation, are being moved to the Wei state, where they are being developed under enemy restrictions. The Japanese have been trying to say that we still have a financial end that has not been fully reached. However, we are blocking it ourselves, which is enough to please the enemy. This government is begging the office to withdraw the order. We believe that you are all Chinese and patriotic and will not please the enemy, but turn the national salvation workers into despair. This government has been conducting anti-Japanese resistance for seven months, and we have exhausted our strength, but we have not dared to be afraid of difficulties and retreat. Heaven has not abandoned China, and we still have this piece of clean land. We hope that the resident Heihe Office of your bank will stick with it to the end. If this government is unable to support it, we will protect your bank's personnel and escape through Russian territory, and we will not allow your bank to suffer any losses. We hope you will quickly telegraph the director and manager of the resident Heihe office to continue their work and not give up. In short, if we cannot restore ordinary remittance, we must at least maintain the status quo. Please be practical and seek profit for it. Chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, Ma Zhanshan, respectfully.

Ministry of Transportation Actively Reorganizing the China Merchants Bureau 128

Revising the Articles of Association for the Debt Consolidation Committee

Consulting the Municipal Government to Ban the Maintenance Association

Regarding the China Merchants Bureau's Board of Directors' request to establish a Debt Consolidation Committee and the recommendation of committee members, the Ministry of Transportation approved the filing yesterday. However, the Ministry believes that the committee's articles of association still require additions and deletions, and the Ministry has revised them, instructing the Board of Directors to comply. The New Voice News Agency's Beijing correspondent has obtained the revised articles of association as follows:

Articles of Association of the Debt Consolidation Committee: The Organizational Articles of Association of the China Merchants Bureau Debt Consolidation Committee. Article 1: The China Merchants Bureau Board of Directors, for the purpose of reorganizing pre-takeover debts, establishes a Debt Consolidation Committee, subordinate to the Board of Directors. Article 2: The powers of the Committee are as follows: (1) Matters concerning the investigation and registration of debts; (2) Matters concerning the review and reporting of debts; (3) Matters concerning the raising and repayment of debts; (4) Matters concerning the review of debt accounts; (5) Other matters related to the reorganization of debts. Article 3: The Committee consists of seven members, selected by resolution of the Board of Directors, four of whom are concurrently serving Board members elected by the Board. Article 4: The Committee members shall elect one member from among the concurrently serving members as the Chairman, who shall regularly attend meetings and preside over committee affairs. Article 5: The Committee shall meet once a week to discuss matters concerning debt reorganization. The Chairman shall report in detail on the progress of the reorganization at each meeting for review and discussion. Article 6: The Chairman shall preside over the Committee meetings. Decisions shall be made with the consent of more than half of all Committee members. If the votes are equal, the Chairman shall have the deciding vote. Article 7: For the convenience of handling affairs, the Committee shall establish the following two groups: (1) Investigation Group, responsible for the investigation and registration of debts, etc.; (2) Review Group, responsible for the review and reporting of debts, etc. Article 8: The Committee may at any time request all documents, contracts, books, registers, forms, etc., of the Bureau related to debts, and may transfer personnel from various departments of the Bureau to handle various matters. Article 9: The Committee may, when it deems necessary, entrust accountants or lawyers to handle the matters stipulated in Article 1 of these Articles of Association, but must obtain the consent of the Board of Directors. Article 10: The Committee's resolutions shall be reported to the Board of Directors for approval and implementation. Article 11: The term of office of the Committee is set at three months, after which it shall be dissolved. Article 12: The Committee may formulate its own detailed rules of procedure, but shall report them to the Board of Directors for record. Article 13: The Committee's expenses shall be approved and allocated by the Board of Directors. Article 14: These Articles of Association shall be implemented after being approved by the Board of Directors and submitted to the Ministry of Transportation for approval.

Banning the Maintenance Association: The Ministry of Transportation believes that since the China Merchants Bureau was nationalized, public opinion has generally been optimistic, believing that the government can fully reorganize and develop it. Even the shareholders are satisfied with the government's method of buying shares at fifty taels per share, and most have actively withdrawn their shares. However, recently, a China Merchants Bureau Shareholder Rights Maintenance Association has opposed the nationalization of the China Merchants Bureau and the government's method of buying shares at fifty taels per share. They have even sent representatives to the Third Plenary Session of the Fourth Central Executive Committee to request the cancellation of the nationalization of the China Merchants Bureau. Recently, the Ministry has received requests from various groups in Shanghai to ban the Maintenance Association and severely punish those who initiated it. The Ministry has now consulted the Shanghai Municipal Government to strictly ban it.

Summary of the Anhui Huai River Embankment Project 132

The Flood Relief Commission Inspects the Upper and Middle Reaches of the Huai River

The special train of the Embankment Inspection Team of the National Government Flood Relief Commission passed through Xuzhou at 3:30 p.m. on the 19th and turned south, arriving in Bengbu at 10:30 p.m. More than fifty local officials, executive and supervisory committee members of the Chamber of Commerce, the Director of the Anhui Huai River Engineering Bureau, and engineers welcomed the team at the station. At 9:00 a.m. on the 20th, a welcome meeting was held at the Anhui Huai River Engineering Bureau, chaired by Director Wang Huzhen. Engineers Wang Xueshu of the 11th Bureau of the Public Works Relief Program and Zhang Chongji of the 13th Bureau reported on the work of the 12 districts of the Anhui Huai River project. Xi Dejiong and Wen Lanting responded. After the meeting, a photograph was taken. The team then went to the wharf and took a small boat to Huaiyuan to inspect the 12th district project, returning to Bengbu at 5:00 p.m. On the 21st, they went to the Wuhe area to inspect the 13th district project, then boarded the train at Linhuai Pass. The Preparatory Director of the Inspection Team, Li Zushen, and his wife had returned to Shanghai by express train at 2:00 a.m. on the 20th due to personal matters. The following is a summary of the engineering overview of the three districts of the Anhui Huai River project and the inspection situation:

(Disaster Situation) Northern Anhui is located in the upper reaches of the Huai River, with high terrain in the west and low terrain in the east. The Hong, Ying, Fei, Wo, Hui, and Tuo Rivers flow down from the northwest in parallel and converge on the Huai River. Every year in both seasons, floods occur due to poor drainage. In July of last year, the continuous rain caused the total amount of rainfall in one month to reach 490 kilometers, which was unprecedented. The water volume of each river increased sharply. The dikes on the south bank of the Huai River were originally incomplete and uneven. As a result, from late June to mid-July, from Huoqiu to Wuhe, the dikes collapsed section by section, flooding 38,000 square miles, causing 38 million yuan in property damage, and more than 40,000 deaths. The number of disaster victims dependent on relief reached 3.9 million. Although emergency relief was distributed by organizations such as the Emergency Relief Association and the J济生会 (Relief Society), it was difficult to reach everyone. Driven by the need to survive, many disaster victims resorted to desperate measures. Gunshots were heard every night in the Bin Huai area.

(Huai River Diversion Project) After the establishment of the Flood Relief Commission's Public Works Relief Office, in view of the tragic disaster in northern Anhui, which was caused by the lack of water conservancy, it was necessary to implement the Huai River Diversion project to permanently eliminate the disaster. However, the plan formulated by the Huai River Diversion Committee involved a huge project that could not be implemented quickly or completed in a short period of time. In order to take into account both providing relief to disaster victims and building water conservancy projects, the office selectively constructed and repaired the dikes that had collapsed in the upper and middle reaches of the Huai River Diversion project, and built new dikes in areas along the Huai River where there were no dikes, surrounding low-lying areas and restoring a certain path for the Huai River. The surveying work was also carried out by the Huai River Diversion Committee, and many engineers were transferred to the project. In addition to building dikes, the office also dredged the North Fei River for 50 miles from Huoqiu to Hongze Lake. The Huai River Diversion project has been largely completed.

(Yin Suo Culvert) At 9:00 a.m. on the 20th, after the welcome meeting was held at the Anhui Huai River Engineering Bureau, the team went to the wharf and took a small boat to Huaiyuan County (23 miles from Bengbu). This place is the mouth of the Wo River into the Huai River. Its north dike is the first section of the 12th district. On the bank of the Huai River, culverts are installed at the mouths of small rivers flowing into the Huai River. Each culvert is named after an ancient person who made meritorious contributions to water management, such as Ximen Bao, Li Bing, Fu Jian, and Du Yu. The one inspected on this day was No. 27, named Yin Suo, which is 112 feet long, making it the longest of all culverts. The culvert is made of three-foot reinforced concrete pipes with three holes. The culvert mouth is equipped with automatic iron doors. When water flows from the inner river into the Huai River, the door opens. When the Huai River water backflows into the inner river, the culvert door closes automatically. The cost is more than 3,224 yuan. The structure of other culverts is the same. After the inspection, the team went to the Tang Huailou at Bai Ruquan, Jing Mountain, west of Huaiyuan County for lunch. After lunch, the team returned to Bengbu on the original boat. In the evening, the Anhui Huai River Engineering Bureau held a banquet. The special train left for Linhuai Pass that night.

(Huai Tuo Dike Project) At 8:30 a.m. on the 21st, the team went to Linhuai Pass wharf and took the Tailai small boat to Wuhe (northeast of Linhuai Pass) to inspect the 13th district project. At 1:30 p.m., the magistrate of Wuhe County, Song Zhinan, and representatives of various agencies and organizations welcomed the team on the shore. After a brief conversation, the team continued to drive to Wulifen to inspect the ten-mile dike project on the north bank of the Huai River in the first section of the district. The dike is four meters wide, which is wider than the original standard of three meters. However, the dike body is loose, and the tracks of ox carts are deeply embedded in two ruts, with dust and sand flying. According to the engineering personnel of the district, this is due to the local soil quality and there is nothing they can do about it. The inner slope is one to two, and an inner slope of one to five should be added to the lower half. Due to time constraints, it has not yet been built. At 3:30 p.m., the boat turned west. At 7:30 p.m., the boat arrived at Linhuai Pass. The special train traveled south at 11:00 p.m. and crossed the Yangtze River on the morning of the 22nd.

(Group Inspection) The original schedule of the Dike Inspection Team was to inspect the upper and lower reaches of the Huai River, then continue to inspect the dike project of the Grand Canal and the dredging project of the Xiangxia River. The team was scheduled to return to Shanghai on the 24th. Later, because the inspection and reception along the way took longer than expected, engineers Zhu Shijun and Xue Zhaoshu went to inspect the 11th district project east and west of Zhengyangguan in the upper reaches of the Huai River. After completing the inspection, they transferred to the Xiangxia River. The remaining personnel inspected the Wuhe dike project and then transferred to Yangzhou and then to Gaoyou and Shaobo to inspect the dike project of the Grand Canal. The team is expected to return to Shanghai around the 24th or 25th. (New Voice News Agency)

Postal Bureau Prefers Special Severance Plan for Postal Workers 133

More Than 800 Chinese Employees Have Resigned

According to the "North China Daily News," it has been learned from reliable sources that the Chinese Postal Administration feels that there is a surplus of personnel after postal workers from the Northeast have entered the customs en masse. In addition, the economic decline has affected the postal service. Now, a special severance plan has been established to encourage long-serving elderly employees to resign voluntarily. To date, it is reported that more than 800 Chinese employees have taken the opportunity to resign. It is expected that more will continue to resign. Several foreign employees have received notices of the severance plan, inviting them to take advantage of this opportunity. As for the severance plan, even those who received special seniority bonuses in 1927 can still receive severance pay based on their years of service. For those who have served for 25 years or less, one month's salary will be given for each year of service. For years exceeding 25 years, half a month's salary will be given for each year. Those who wish to return to their home country will also be given first-class travel expenses and a generous allowance for the time spent on the journey. During this period, they will still be paid their full salary.

Japanese Naval Training Fleet Arrives in Shanghai 134

Will Return to Japan at Noon Tomorrow

The Japanese naval training fleet, "Yakumo" and "Pan-te," led by Vice Admiral Hyakutake, arrived in Shanghai from Lushun and Qingdao. Yesterday morning at 7:30, "Pan-te" was in the lead, followed by "Yakumo," sailing from Wusong into the Huangpu River, where they docked at the Mitsubishi Wharf. The Japanese Consul in Shanghai, Ishishe Tadashi, Rear Admiral, Counselor Yokotake, Secretary Horiuchi, Administrative Committee Chairman Yasui, Funatsu, and Yoneiri all went to the "Pan-te" at 10:00 to pay their respects to Hyakutake. Hyakutake told the representatives of the Japanese community that he had come to Shanghai on January 18 this year and did not expect the war in Shanghai to break out ten days later. He felt very emotional about this. This time, naval officer students came to visit the Shanghai battlefield, which showed the intensity of the war at that time. Chief Accountant Morihisa Kichiji said that the fleet left Japan on November 19 and first went to Manchuria, where they met with Puyi. However, because the weather was too cold there, they could not stay long. Now that they have come to Shanghai, they will return to Japan at noon on the 24th. They are scheduled to arrive at the Sasebo Naval Port on December 4. The long-distance training is scheduled to take place in late January, departing from Japan for Europe, traveling 18,000 nautical miles around Europe and the South Pacific Islands, and then returning to Japan.

Salary Arrears and Raises for Employees of the Two Railways Resolved 135

A portion of the train service employees of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway did not have their seniority raises from 1932 approved, even though other departments had already announced them. Therefore, the entire organization, the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Comrades Salary Arrears and Raises Delegation, repeatedly petitioned the Railway Bureau, but to no avail. After the new Director, Huang Boqiao, took office, the delegation held a meeting at Jiaxing Station the night before last, resolving to notify the authorities to provide a definite reply by 6:00 p.m. yesterday, otherwise they would be forced to strike and not be responsible for the consequences. The situation was extremely serious for a time. It is now learned that the case has been resolved. Yesterday, the authorities of the two railways received instructions from the Ministry of Railways to approve the payment of salary arrears and raises. The Railway Bureau immediately notified the trade unions of the two railways to inform the delegation. After learning the facts, the trade unions immediately sent an urgent telegram: "Urgent, Jiaxing Station to Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo to Comrades Salary Arrears and Raises Delegation Consulate, and to all station team members: The case of the raise of 17 in this city was telegraphed yesterday. The Ministry's order has been approved today and is now being processed by the Railway Bureau. It will be announced soon. Please inform all members not to be impatient. This association is willing to take full responsibility, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Trade Union Council". In addition, Councilors Min Luoheng and staff member Liu Junming were sent to Jiaxing yesterday afternoon to attend the delegation's 6:00 p.m. meeting to provide guidance and report.

Drawing Donations to Help Northeast Refugees 138

Purchase a Chinese Typewriter

Can Donate 30 Yuan Method

The China Industrial Development Company, No. 9 Hankou Road in this city, in view of the fact that the three northeastern provinces have suffered from Japanese bandits, and the compatriots have been displaced, and the wailing of refugees is everywhere, and now that there is wind and snow, hunger and cold, the miserable situation is unbearable, the people in the rear cannot bear to wait for their death, so they took advantage of the Northeastern Refugee Relief Fair held in the New World to sell the company's patented national brand new Chinese typewriter, originally priced at 300 yuan, to customers at a 10% discount, and donate 30 yuan per unit to Northeast refugees, and deliver the money to the conference when it is sold, but the company deeply feels that the Northeastern Refugee Relief Fair has a limited time, and if the community needs to delay the purchase, it will not help, but the company remembers the refugees in the three provinces, not wanting to be behind, so it has devised a method, deeply hoping that all those who intend to buy a Chinese typewriter can pay a deposit of 30 yuan first, and the company will pay the money to the conference, so that the refugees in the three northeastern provinces will get more to eat and wear, and the customers will not lose anything, this kind of enthusiastic righteous act is worthy of admiration, I hope that all sectors will rise up quickly, if you have any questions or requests for samples, please contact Wang Jianxin, the sports group of the New World Fair.

Construction Costs Paid from the Reconstruction Public Bond

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, in view of the lack of a complete municipal hospital in the city, has repeatedly requested the municipal government to allocate funds to establish one as soon as possible, but because of the city's financial constraints, it has not been realized. It is now learned that the city's wartime reconstruction public bond has been issued, and the construction of a municipal hospital is also one of the uses of the bond. Therefore, Health Director Li Tingan has discussed the construction of a municipal hospital with the Municipal Public Works Bureau, and it is learned that the construction site of the municipal hospital is in the city center.

Ji Jiannan, Sun Wenyi, Shi Zongtang, and Si Ren carried letters and went to the Public Works Department to request the board of directors of the department to reconsider. They were received by Mr. He De Kui, the meeting organizer. After the representatives stated their intentions, Mr. He replied that he would submit the suggestions for reconsideration and then reply. The representatives then resigned. The letter to the Public Works Department is recorded as follows: "Dear Sirs, Although the news of the telephone price increase was disclosed in the Chinese newspapers in July, the measures were never announced in advance, and the company required users to retrospectively compensate for the new price, which has never happened before and is inconsistent with reason and law. Moreover, 'No Retroactivity' is a universally recognized legal principle. Our association sent another letter to your department on November 15, requesting that you accept the public opinion of the majority of citizens and re-set a fair new price, but the case has been delayed until now and has not been followed. If it is not resolved soon, it will inevitably lead to an unstable situation."

Suddenly Entered Wuben Dormitory

Heard Breathing in the Dark

The thief, Zhang Liying, is 29 years old, wearing a blue striped serge cheongsam, gray sheepskin gloves, black silk stockings, and mao ge round-mouth shoes, and lives on Lan Ni Du Avenue, Pudong. She turned to the school to look for someone and denied stealing. According to the representative of Wuben Girls' Middle School, Yuan Wei, a native of Wujin, is 41 years old and serves as the school's general affairs officer. He said that the woman sneaked into dormitory room No. 13 on the upper floor when the school was dismissed, and stole a woolen sweater from Qin Qiuying's bed No. 1 and a woolen overcoat from Shi Jiying's bed No. 6 in the same room. At that time, Shi Jiying went upstairs after dinner and heard breathing in the dark when she entered the bedroom. She shined a flashlight and saw the woman sneaking into the bedroom, pretending to be a student of the school. She found the stolen clothes on the spot. Because she was caught, she threw them under bed No. 4. Please punish her according to the law. After checking the confession, Inspector Chen ordered the woman and the woolen overcoat and evidence to be sent to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau today for handling according to law.

Quarterly Report of the Joint Savings Society 147

155th Time

The Joint Savings Society is jointly established by the Yien Yieh Commercial Bank, the Kin Cheng Banking Corporation, the Chung Nan Bank, and the Continental Bank. It specializes in issuing banknotes of the Chung Nan Bank. In accordance with the Society's issuance charter, banknotes are issued with full reserves. Cash reserves must be at least 60%, and guarantee reserves must be up to 40%. It is announced once a week after verification by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The 155th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve of December 17, 21, is recorded as follows: Value of banknotes in circulation: 25,140,357 yuan; Total amount of reserves: 25,140,357 yuan, including cash reserves of 19,221,457 yuan and guarantee reserves of 5,914,900 yuan.

Five Provinces and Cities Interconnect Vehicles, Minhang Adds New Ferry 150

Can Carry Ten Cars and One Hundred and Twenty People at a Time

Costing 80,000 Yuan, to Be Completed in April Next Year

Regarding the interconnection of automobiles in the five provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Beijing, and Shanghai, the National Economic Commission and the five provinces and cities each sent a representative to form a Transportation Committee, and convened the first meeting in the capital on March 17. The representative of this city is Tan Boying, the chief of the Fourth Section of the Municipal Public Works Bureau. Mr. Tan returned to Shanghai on the 19th. Yesterday, a reporter from the Central News Agency asked Mr. Tan about the details of the transportation meeting. The answer is as follows: My country's provinces are vast, transportation is inconvenient, and languages and customs are different, which can easily lead to misunderstandings and disputes. For example, Sichuan has had endless disputes over the years, which is clear evidence. In recent years, the central government has promoted and urged the construction of highways in the five provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Beijing, and Shanghai, sparing no effort. Recently, it will be promoted to reach seven provinces, but after the roads are built, the management methods of the transportation vehicles must be unified to avoid the suffering of asking about customs when entering the country and to achieve mutual contact. This is the reason for the establishment of the Transportation Committee of the five provinces and cities. On the 17th of this month, the preparatory office of the National Economic Commission convened the first meeting of the Transportation Committee of the five provinces and cities in Beijing. The organization of the association is that the five provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Beijing, and Shanghai and the preparatory office of the National Economic Commission each send an expert as a member, and the representative of the preparatory office of the National Economic Commission is the standing committee member. A meeting is held in a different place every two months. Its important significance lies in: ㈠ Unifying the colors and styles of various transportation vehicle licenses,

㈡ Unifying the traffic signs along the way, ㈢ Unifying the traffic management methods and regulations, ㈣ Unifying the examination methods for drivers of various motor vehicles, ㈤ If a car driver causes an accident in his own province or city, the license will be revoked and other provinces and cities will be notified at the same time to avoid fraudulent receipt. The above sections are intended to increase traffic efficiency and reduce the pain of travel. In the future, the promotion of the whole country will have a great impact. The members sent by the provinces and cities this time have the same intention and cooperate sincerely. There are as many as 22 proposals, which were completely resolved within 10 hours. All resolutions are reasonable, so they can be effectively implemented and take effect very quickly. The Japanese criticized our country as an unorganized country, which can be defeated without attacking. As far as this city's position is concerned, it attaches great importance to the Shanghai-Hangzhou highway, because Chinese and Western travelers travel frequently, and the relationship is very important. In addition to ensuring safety, convenience and speed must be taken into account, especially the reform of the Minhang ferry should not be delayed. The design of the ferry is undertaken by this city after being jointly recommended by the provinces and cities. Shanghai has the largest number of cars in the country. Every Saturday and Sunday, many people go to Hangzhou for sightseeing. The existing ferry can carry two cars at a time. If there are 100 cars, the last car will have to wait for two hours before crossing the river, which is very inconvenient for travelers. It is even more difficult to cope with the spring floods. Therefore, the bureau plans to run a large ferry at both ends, which can carry ten cars at a time and carry one hundred and twenty passengers at the same time. It can transport 150 cars per hour. The boat is 90 feet long and 23 feet wide. The diesel engine has 120 horsepower. Even heavy objects weighing 20 tons can be loaded on the deck. It takes only one and a half minutes to cross the river. The bureau has submitted the drawings and specifications of the ferry to the Transportation Committee of the five provinces and cities for approval, and construction will start soon. It may be completed in April next year. In the future, when it is completed, it will be the first and most modern car ferry in the East. The new ferry costs a total of 80,000 yuan. After the new ferry is completed, the existing Minhang ferry will be transferred to Dangtu County, Anhui Province, for use. The construction cost of the new ferry will be allocated by the National Economic Commission for more than 25,000 yuan and 30,000 yuan will be allocated from the surcharge for the interconnection of automobiles in the five provinces and cities. The remaining amount will be offset from the car ferry fund and handed over to the Jiangsu Construction Department for handling, and the Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau is requested to assist in handling.

Institute of Forensic Medicine Examines Corpse and Discovers Cadaverine Morphine 151

The First Discovery in China

The Institute of Forensic Medicine recently accepted a case from Zhenjiang and discovered cadaverine morphine in the corpse, thus redressing the injustice. At first, there were two men and women in Zhenjiang who were not formally married, and the woman was addicted to coal dust. Suddenly, the woman died, and the woman's family sued the man in court, saying that she had been abused and died from smoking. At first, the hospital examined and proved that she died of lung disease. Then, the forensic doctor in Zhenjiang re-examined and found a lot of morphine. The prosecutor transferred the case to the court. (The judge believed that there were many doubts in this case, and re-examined a piece of liver left over from the dissection and examination, only as big as a finger, and the skin and bones of the feet, and transferred them to the Institute of Forensic Medicine for further examination. The institute was accused of smoking, so it first examined opium acid, and after repeated examinations, it was not found. Then, it re-examined and found a lot of morphine in this small piece of liver, only as big as a finger. It tried to extract the morphine and inject it into a live rabbit, but there was no change. Only then did it recognize that it was cadaverine morphine, not plant morphine, because plant morphine must cause fainting and death when injected into a live rabbit. Cadaverine morphine is produced by the decay of animal corpses, and the discovery of cadaverine morphine is a new discovery.

Shanghai Municipal Council Considers Improving Film Censorship 152

In order to improve the film censorship method, the Shanghai Municipal Council previously appointed an investigation committee. The results of the investigation have been prepared and reported. The Municipal Council then issued the report to various departments for review and sent their opinions to the Security Committee for review. At the meeting of the committee on the 9th of this month, the chief of the police department stated that most of the criticisms of film censorship were criticisms of the nature of the film, not the standards of censorship. As for the investigation committee's proposal that the censorship committee should have the final decision-making power, according to the general manager, the Municipal Council has no right to grant this responsibility, so it is difficult to implement.

Since the investigation committee did not object to the current system, the police committee believed that there was no need for drastic reforms. In addition, it has never been difficult to recruit people to serve as volunteer censors, so it is difficult to agree to pay them. However, the proposal to set up a preview room seems feasible for the convenience of centralizing censorship work. Mr. Bolton also sent a letter stating that he is willing to provide equipment, but it is not known how much it is needed. He should be asked to explain everything in detail again, and whether the first branch of the Health Bureau can be converted into a projection hall is also waiting for the investigation report. In view of the above circumstances, the committee did not make specific recommendations on the report of the investigation committee, but expressed that any proposals that the chief of the police department believes can be implemented may be adopted. The minutes of the committee have been approved by the board of directors at the meeting on the 21st.

Marriage Dispute Between Yang Fansheng's Younger Sister and Chauffeur 153

Chauffeur Sues Yang for Obstruction of Freedom

Yang Says Chauffeur Fabricated Accusations

Yang Fansheng, the owner of Bao Da Ginseng Shop at No. 75 Fengsheng Lane, Mulou Road, was sued by his former chauffeur, Li Gengfu, for obstruction of freedom. After being tried by Judge Fu of the First Special District Court, the defendant's lawyer requested that the case not be accepted because the date of the crime (February 28) stated in the plaintiff's accusation was before the promulgation of the amnesty decree. Judge Liu ordered that the case be investigated before the trial. The hearing continued yesterday afternoon. First, Li Gengfu stated the intent of the lawsuit, stating that he was hired as a chauffeur by the defendant in December of the previous year. Yang Fazhen, the defendant's sixteen-year-old younger sister, always used me as a driver whenever she took a car. Over time, she gradually inquired about my family background. Because she knew that I was not married, Miss Yang said that she would be my matchmaker. From then on, she often went out with me and sent me love letters from time to time,

Willing to Marry Me as Wife I refused at first, saying that you have a mother and a brother, how can you be independent? Miss Yang said that if her mother did not agree, she would break away from the relationship. Now that marriage is free, how can her brother restrain her? She also gave me her photo, vowing to grow old together. I also told her that the difference between rich and poor is too great, and I am afraid it will be difficult to achieve my wish. Miss Yang then advised me to change my career and gave me funds to pay for social expenses. Later, I learned that the position of business director of the Zhaoshang Bureau's Tunan ship could be obtained. After discussing it with Miss Yang, she asked her mother and brother to give me a ten-thousand-yuan promissory note. The defendant also sent a letter to Yue Zhenbao, the owner of Taichang Wood Shop, asking him to recommend me. So I took the job on December 25th of last year. I never expected that the Japanese invaders suddenly invaded Shanghai shortly after taking over the job. The war had a great impact on the shipping industry. After the ceasefire, the Tunan ship was used for military service again, resulting in huge losses. The loans I borrowed from relatives and friends could not be repaid when they were due, and some

have been sued. After I became the comprador of the ship, I still lived in the defendant's house. On the night of February 28th of this year, two people suddenly came to the defendant's smoking room upstairs. After the defendant explained my name to the two people, one of them took out a gun and ordered me to return the letters and photos given by Miss Yang. I refused at first. The other person cursed and wanted to search my pockets. I dared not resist, so I handed over a photo and seven letters in my pocket and drawer to the two people to the defendant. After the two people left, I reasoned with the defendant. The defendant said that you want my sister, but it is impossible. At that time, the defendant's mother also arrived, saying that the Yang family had always been decent,

Urging Me Not to Disclose They still agreed to maintain my business, but now it is just lip service. Since the defendant has broken his promise, I have no way to deal with the debts I owe, so I have to sue, etc. When asked, the defendant Yang Fansheng testified that my family has always been very disciplined, and there is no such thing. The plaintiff is purely fabricating accusations. Otherwise, please order him to provide evidence. Since the plaintiff has no evidence now, I don't want to argue too much, etc. Judge Liu then asked Li about the incident on February

28th If there were any other witnesses, Li replied that Zhang Zugen and Yu Qingfeng knew about it. The two witnesses were summoned for questioning. According to Zhang, he used to be a tea servant in Yang's house and quit after the Dragon Boat Festival. Yu used to be Yang's chauffeur, but both said that they heard a quarrel upstairs and went upstairs to see, but the door was closed when they arrived at the door, so they did not know what was taken away, etc. After the lawyers on both sides argued, the court ordered the verdict to be announced on the afternoon of the 24th of this month.

High Court as in a Funny Play

Record of the Trial of Tan Ying's Appeal Case 154

Tan Ying Paints Eyebrows and Applies Powder, Displays a Charming Demeanor

Tan's Mother Refuses the Original Verdict and Kneels Down, Weeping Loudly

Gu Baosen Secretly Remembers Tan's Words as Conclusive

Both Sides' Lawyers Engage in Fierce Arguments in Court

Tan Ying, a Shanghai Lianhua actress who also plays the role of a fallen woman, accused landlord Gu Baosen of rape. As a result of age issues, the Shanghai court ruled Gu not guilty. Gu then filed a countersuit in the original court accusing Tan Ying and her mother of false accusation. The court sentenced Tan Wangshi and Tan Ying to two months' imprisonment with a two-year reprieve and dismissed the related civil suit. Dissatisfied, Tan Ying and her mother hired lawyers Weng Zhifan and Wang Jian to appeal to the Jiangsu High Court. Yesterday (the 22nd) afternoon, a summons was issued to begin the trial. Respondent Gu Baosen also hired lawyers Liu Zhen, Wang Peiyuan, and Xu Qinfu as his representatives. When Tan Ying reported for duty, she wore a teal-colored fur-collared red-lined coat, a blue cloth cheongsam, beige socks, and flesh-colored embroidered shoes, with painted eyebrows and powdered face, displaying a charming demeanor. Her mother also wore a long, floor-length dress and a shawl. While in the waiting room, onlookers came and went, eager to catch a glimpse of the star's beauty. Tan Ying was not at all shy, chattering about her feelings. Gu Baosen, on the other hand, tried to avoid attention after arriving at the court. The case was heard by the First Criminal Division Judge Li Mian and Judge Lin Zhezhang, with Prosecutor Zhu Wenzhuo and Clerk Wu Daquan recording the proceedings. Due to the large number of cases, the trial was delayed until 4 p.m. and adjourned after 5 p.m. Tan Wangshi knelt down four times in court, crying and pleading. The lawyers for both sides clashed fiercely over speaking rights, turning the courtroom into a farcical scene. The court announced that a retrial would be held after further investigation. The detailed circumstances are as follows:

Now, the eight characters are in the mountain temple, placed in front of the Bodhisattva Guanyin. (At this time, Tan Wangshi knelt on the ground and cried loudly.) (Answer): Yes. (Question): How can you tell? (Answer): They are for my daughter. (Question): Go to Guanqian, pay two cents, any fortune teller can write them. (Note: Guanqian is a place name in Suzhou, where there are many fortune tellers.) (Answer): We women don't lie. If we lie, we are willing to face legal action. Baosen raped my daughter and should be punished. Now, I have been sentenced to imprisonment, it's really too bitter.

The issue of lawyers appearing in court should not be debated until the appropriate time. The court then adjourned.

Wu Huaichun Accused by a Woman from Changshu

Raped Young Daughter to Death, Then Raped Eldest Daughter and Abandoned Her 155

The facts are extremely complicated... The judge hopes for a reconciliation

Wu Huaichun, a wealthy businessman from Suzhou who owns many properties in Shanghai, resides at No. 24, Lane 5, Ximen Road in the French Concession, and has established Yinyu Company there to manage rental accounts. He is now being sued in the Second Special District Court by Shi Chenshi, a woman from Changshu, through her lawyer, for criminally raping her fifteen-year-old daughter Lingyu to death and, while Lingyu was ill, raping her nineteen-year-old eldest daughter Jinghua, and then abandoning her shortly after. She is requesting that he be severely punished according to the law and is also filing a related civil suit. The case has already been opened for trial, and the parties involved, as well as physical evidence and photos, have already been published in newspapers and are well known to everyone. The case was scheduled for a continued hearing yesterday afternoon. The plaintiff, Shi Chenshi and her daughter Shi Jinghua, arrived at the court with their lawyers Wu Peng, Hu Jue, and He Yijun to report for the hearing at 2 p.m. The first defendant, Wu Huaichun, also arrived with his defense lawyer Pan Cheng. The second defendant, Fan Guilin, was represented by lawyer Zhu Dianqing. Fan's concubine, Fan Wengshi, also arrived on time. At the third ringing of the bell, Judge Li Changnian and Clerk Wang Baoxun took their seats in the Second Criminal Court for the hearing.

The audience was packed, with no empty seats. After the judge opened the court, the bailiff called the parties to the bar. Shi Chenshi stood in the defendant's box with her hair cut short, wearing a black woolen cheongsam. Shi Jinghua's hair was disheveled, and she was wearing a black fur-collared coat. Wu Huaichun was wearing a gray crepe robe and glasses. The lawyers for both sides also appeared in court one after another. The judge first asked the plaintiff and defendants their names, ages, origins, and occupations. Then, he asked Fan Wengshi, "Who are you to the defendant Fan Guilin?" I know the details of this matter, so I came to the court on behalf of Fan to await questioning." Plaintiff's lawyer Hu Jue stood up and said, "The second defendant, Fan Guilin, dared not appear in court and sent Wengshi to appear on his behalf, but a criminal defendant cannot be replaced by someone else. Please ask the court to order Weng to withdraw." Defendant's lawyer Pan countered, "Whether a party withdraws is within the court's jurisdiction and cannot be claimed by the plaintiff's lawyer." The two sides argued fiercely. The judge then ordered Fan Wengshi to withdraw to the audience and ordered both sides' lawyers to stop arguing. He then asked both parties, "This case has been postponed for a long time, have you ever reconciled outside the court?" Both sides answered that they had not reconciled. Because she met Fan Guilin, who was from the same hometown, she stayed at Fan's house. We knew that Fan was in the candy business and ran a shop. Later, Guilin said to my sister, "You are poor and can't afford to study. I will hire a teacher to teach you singing." On June 29th of the lunar calendar last year, she was raped by Wu at Fan's house." My mother and I were in the countryside, and my sister also told us in a letter. conspired together." Chenshi also said, "I didn't know at first. Lingyu told me when she was dying." The judge asked the defendant Wu Huaichun, "Did you hear what the plaintiff said?" The family said that Dr. Zhu Hegao had seen her and it didn't help. They wanted to send her to the hospital, but Lingyu was afraid and didn't want to go. Chenshi and Lingyu moved in on April 23rd. I only took care of the medical expenses. The meals were provided by the Fan family. Then, her mother asked me to borrow 300 yuan, saying that after paying the Fan family back, they would no longer have to live at the Fan's house. I also agreed to lend it to her and paid it back on May 9th. Later, her mother said to me that because I had spent so much money, she was willing to send Lingyu to me as a concubine. At that time, I replied that the first thing was to treat the illness, and when she was better, the second thing was to go back to the countryside to study. came to Shanghai to visit her and take care of her. I also asked Dr. Zhang Chongmin to examine her, who said that she had reached the third stage of lung disease. Chenshi called me and said to me that the person always belongs to you. All funeral matters should be handled by you. Reader's Advisor

Rural Education 156

In the first semester of last year, I had an idea to write a book on the rural economy of China. I had completed more than 70,000 words of the introduction, but unfortunately, the January 28th Incident destroyed it along with the school. However, this idea has always been in my mind and has never disappeared. Therefore, I always pay close attention to anything related to this issue. Undoubtedly, in the rural problem, which is also the Chinese problem, "universal education" is the most urgent issue at present. According to statistics, 93% of the population is illiterate. Now, the general educated people can feel the importance of this issue and are working hard, especially the efforts of the Popular Education Promotion Association in Ding County and the Shanghai Chinese Vocational Education Society, which must be regarded as a ray of dawn for the future of rural education in China.

However, on the other hand, how much effectiveness can universal compulsory education have in rural areas? In the current environment, I am a bit skeptical. According to experience, only a very small number of people attend free schools. I think that free schools in rural areas are likely to conflict with work if they teach during the day: at night, after a day of labor, after dinner, they fall asleep. After working for twelve hours, it is impossible and should not be asked to use their brains for two hours. Even if we only refer to school-age children, according to what I have heard in conversations in rural areas, they are often unwilling to send their children to school.

The reason is that in the current economic environment, it is so difficult to maintain a family's livelihood with one person's income. Therefore, in our area, when children are eight or nine years old, they go out to look after cattle, and daughters are mostly sent to be adopted daughters-in-law. Because more consumption by one person means less production by one person on the other hand; children of eight or nine years old cannot be expected to produce, but because they are given to herd cattle, their own living problems can be solved without the need for their parents to maintain them. In most rural families, even the livelihood of one child is difficult to maintain. The increase in the number of orphanages is a very superficial proof. Therefore, even if compulsory education is implemented, how can it be possible to voluntarily send children to school? Even if it is possible to implement compulsory education, how will the resulting livelihood problems be solved? "Studying is okay, but how about life?" I often hear similar conversations.

Let's take a step back and allow rural children to enter school at the age of six and study until the age of ten. This is easier to do in practice. But what can be gained from these four years of education? What's more, often at the age of eight at most, their fathers and brothers must also make them a part of the production?

However, the urgent need to popularize education is an urgent issue in all aspects. Difficulties must be overcome, but how to overcome them? Let us assume that the implementation of universal education has a considerable solution in terms of funding, but how can we achieve the goal of universal education? How can we make fathers and brothers willing to send their children to school without conflicting with their livelihoods? These are all problems.

To answer the above questions, we can say very beautifully that this is an inevitable phenomenon under private ownership, so we must break the current economic organization in order to achieve it. But this is a bit too ambitious, and the immediate urgent problem must be broken immediately. Theoretical insights must also take into account reality.

I feel that this is not just my personal problem, and I am afraid that everyone who has been engaged in rural education has this doubt. Therefore, I dare to make a request to the teacher to answer it. If it can be made public, it is also what I deeply hope for. (Letter from Bao Zuxuan)

Editor's Note: The questions raised by Bao are indeed worthy of public discussion. We will temporarily put them forward for public discussion.

Women and Occupations 157

I have been married for three years and now have a two-year-old child. My husband works as a clerk in a foreign firm. Because there are few people in our family and the expenses are light, our life is quite comfortable. ::: I always thought that living this mundane life was too boring. ::: Women should also have occupations. ::: Although I studied for a few years before I got married, I can't say I have any professional skills. So I plan to go back to school, so that I can find a suitable job in the future. I told him this idea, but unexpectedly he strongly opposed it. He said that once a woman is married, she does not need a career, "washing clothes, cooking, and giving birth to children" is her career. Sir, isn't this too insulting to women? I argued with him several times, but to no avail; but the money is in his hands, what other way do I have besides asking him for it? Therefore, I feel the need for economic independence even more. )::: Sir, what do you think is best? (Message from Ms. Ao Wanying)

(Answer) "Women should have occupations" is a brilliant idea: it is indeed ten thousand times higher than the current women who only know how to consume and cannot produce. The lady's request is of course legitimate. However, our advocacy of women's occupations or women's economic independence is not all-encompassing. The general opinion is that women's occupations or women's economic independence seems to take a confrontational meaning towards men; this is really a misunderstanding. To put it correctly, negatively opposing women's dependent life, like parasites increasing social consumption, and positively advocating women's participation in social production, whether directly or indirectly. We hope that women will participate in production with the spirit of human mutual assistance, but we never want women to have a mentality of competing or refusing to show weakness. On this point, we should completely eliminate the concept of gender differences for thousands of years. We are all just people: we are just doing our best. If we must compete to do men's things, and abandon the things that women should do or that only women can do, then this is contrary to the basic principle of production | the principle of division of labor. As for "washing clothes, cooking, and giving birth to children" being a woman's occupation, it is indeed "insulting to women" in wording, but not in meaning. "Washing clothes, cooking, and giving birth to children" are indeed women's affairs, but these things are not necessarily lowly. Managing the household and the head of state governing national affairs do not differ in terms of the significance of production, and may even be more fundamental. Children's education is even more related to the future of the country and the nation. Unfortunately, the current school education only has the function of enlightenment, and completely lacks the function of edification: then, who can bear this great responsibility other than ordinary mothers? If a woman can wholeheartedly educate her children and make them perfect citizens, it is much greater than abandoning her children to earn a salary of a few tens of dollars a month. If the lady understands the greatness and importance of her own responsibility, she will definitely be interested. Moreover, now that she is in charge of household affairs and the child is still young, she naturally feels economically well-off. Once she goes to school, she will inevitably have to hire servants at home, plus

the expense of tuition, which adds two burdens out of thin air, which is very uneconomical. If you feel the need to study, you may wish to prepare books and study on your own in your spare time. In short, the spirit of mutual assistance is the key to the success of all undertakings; "arguing with him" is useless to everyone.

Zhu Suixuan, a Rascal from Yancheng, Impersonates a Section Chief of the China Merchants Bureau 158

Sets up an office in the Tingzi (pavilion) building

Introduces jobs to swindle movement expenses

Many photos of the swindled people are copied out

There are even congratulatory letters from prostitutes in Yancheng

Zhu Suixuan, a native of Yancheng, is 26 years old, with the alias Tie Mei. He was a rascal in academic circles in his hometown, addicted to prostitution and gambling, and despised by the masses, making it difficult for him to gain a foothold in society. At the beginning of this month, he came to Shanghai and rented a pavilion room on the upper floor of No. 674 Dongyalv Road to set up a fraudulent institution. He posted a sign on the door saying "China Merchants Company Office, No Entry for Idlers", and printed business cards, on which he wrote "Member of the Executive Committee and Chief of the General Affairs Section of the Central China Merchants Bureau". He wore a Western suit and leather shoes, looking very handsome. He falsely claimed that he could introduce positions such as inspectors and dockworkers of the China Merchants Bureau, with high salaries. More than 20 people, including Wang Yuejiang and Yin Zhaofeng, were fooled by him, and the introduction fees swindled from them amounted to hundreds of gold. The day before yesterday at noon, Yin Zheng hosted a dinner for Zhu and invited a friend surnamed Zhang to accompany him. He also told him that he had been recommended by Section Chief Zhu to the position of inspector of the Central China Merchants Bureau and would be able to start work soon. It was said that this was a good position and would bring considerable benefits in the future. He had already given him 40 yuan for movement expenses. Zhang saw that Zhu Suixuan was a slippery character, and that the office of the Chief of the General Affairs Section of the China Merchants Bureau was so large, how could it be set up in a pavilion room? He was being deceived, so he secretly reported to the Jiaxing Road Police Station, which sent Chinese detective Xu Yongyuan, together with Western detective Ke Laosi, to arrest Zhu. In the pavilion room, they copied out a wooden square seal of the China Merchants Company, a stack of introduction coupons, the defendant's business card and a roll of newspaper clippings of news about the reorganization of the China Merchants Bureau, as well as more than 20 photos of people who entrusted him to introduce jobs, all of which were taken to the police station. The police chief ordered him to be detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, described the situation in detail, and said that according to the appearance of the people who were swindled by the defendant in this case, there were 22 people, but only five people had been brought to justice, and the rest could not be traced and summoned. He presented all the evidence and asked for an extension to investigate the matter in detail. According to Wang Yuejiang, a native of Yancheng, who was involved in the case, he knew the defendant as a fellow villager. On the 4th of this month, he met him on Yangshupu Road and asked him where he was working. He replied that he was not. He said that he could find him a job as an inspector of the China Merchants Bureau, but he needed 30 to 40 gold for movement expenses. He pleaded with him to reduce it. As a result, he sent 20 yuan on the 11th to the defendant's pavilion room office. He said that he did not need to take a photo and gave him his business card and his portrait as a receipt, and promised that he could go to work in the bureau on the 15th. When the deadline arrived, he made excuses to delay it, and then he knew he had been deceived. Yesterday, he reported to the police station. According to Yin Zhaofeng, a native of Taizhou, he did not know the defendant and was introduced by his nephew surnamed Chen. He paid a total of 40 yuan for movement expenses to fill an inspector position and was fooled by him. According to Wei Mingde, a native of Gaoyou, the defendant promised to introduce him to work as a worker at the China Merchants Bureau dock and was swindled out of 20 yuan. According to Chen Liansan, a native of Tongzhou, he lived with the defendant. He said that he was working at the China Merchants Bureau and had an office in the pavilion room. In the past, he saw that his friends who came were all well-dressed. He claimed to be introducing odd jobs at the dock and swindled him out of only two yuan. According to Wang Yaosheng, a native of Yancheng, he also lived with the defendant. He made excuses to introduce business to me and swindled me out of half a month's food expenses. When questioned, the defendant confessed that the seals, business cards, etc. were all bought from old goods stalls, and the rest of his供支吾, 沈炳榮推事向其詳詰良久, 不肯直言, 遂諭仍還押, 改期再核. The police station requested that the various victims of the fraud report to the Jiaxing Road Police Station. A letter from Yun Lan, a famous prostitute in Yancheng, was also found in the defendant's pavilion room, saying that she had come to congratulate him on his appointment as "my dear brother's" glorious position, which was quite a strange story.

Rent Should Be Collected According to the National Calendar Standard 160

Civil Judgment of the First Special Court

Appeal of Jardine Matheson Dismissed

Jardine Matheson of Nanjing Road in this port previously claimed that Lang Jingji, the owner of the semi-Tianbao Zhai store at No. 84 Jiujiang Road, did not pay the rent according to the lunar calendar calculated by the bank. Shen Licheng, the manager of the bank, filed a lawsuit with the Civil Summary Court of the First Special District Court in the capacity of legal representative according to the principle that the law is not retroactive. After the court tried the case, it ruled that since the lunar calendar was issued by law, the rent should be collected according to the National Calendar. Jardine Matheson declared its disagreement in court and hired lawyers Wu Kaisheng and Tang Huaiqun to appeal to the Special District Local Court. It is now known that the case has been heard by the three judges of the court, Li Hu, Yang Peng, and Shen Hong, and the judgment result has been announced, Jardine Matheson's appeal was dismissed, and all rent collection should still be based on the National Calendar standard. The court's reasons for the judgment are excerpted as follows: The undisputed fact is that the appellant has not paid the rent for six months from February to July of this year. The dispute is whether the calculation method should be based on the National Calendar or the lunar calendar. This court has found that the lunar calendar has been explicitly abolished by the National Government, and the general commerce has also switched to the National Calendar. The appellant has failed to independently uphold a different view and still uses the lunar calendar to collect rent. The original trial was calculated according to the National Calendar and ordered the appellant to repay 432.5 taels of silver, which is not inappropriate. The statement that the law is not retroactive is for vested rights. In this case, the appellant claimed to switch to the National Calendar in accordance with laws and regulations and did not pay the rent calculated according to the lunar calendar to the appellant, so there is no retroactivity to speak of. Further investigation found that the appellant's failure to pay rent was due to the unresolved issue of switching to the National Calendar, which is different from ordinary rent arrears.

New Regulations for Riding Motorized Bicycles 164

From January 1 next year, the regulations for motorized bicycle (two-wheeled and three-wheeled) licenses of the Public Concession will be modified in several aspects. One is that an enamel round plate should be added to the top of the three-wheeled vehicle license plate. The other is that the vehicles should be inspected by the Police Department on time. In addition, two-wheeled vehicles are only allowed to carry one person in addition to the driver. That person should sit sideways behind the driver and the seat must be firmly installed.

This Port

Recent Overview of School Hygiene Jointly Run by the Two Bureaus 171

The first phase of work can be completed by the end of the year

The second and third phases of work will begin next spring

The school hygiene jointly run by the Municipal Health Bureau and the Education Bureau is originally divided into three phases. The first phase of work has begun at the beginning of this month and will be completed by the end of this year. The second and third phases of work will continue next year. The plan and current status of the work are explored below.

Past History School hygiene has been considered one of the main tasks since the establishment of the Health Bureau. Therefore, the handling has never been interrupted. However, since the January 28th Shanghai War this spring, most schools have suffered losses, and the Health Bureau's funds have also been very tight, so the work was temporarily suspended. Later, the former director, Hu Hongyi, believed that the work was very important, so he disturbed the restoration and drafted a plan to be implemented next spring. After the new director, Li Ting'an, took office after Director Hu's tragic car accident, he felt that health facilities should not be delayed and still consulted with the Education Bureau according to the original plan of the former director Hu and actively prepared for it, so it was implemented from last month.

Implementation Plan The facilities of school hygiene must be popularized, but due to economic relations, it is divided into three phases. The first phase is the municipal schools in the three districts of the city, Gaoyang Zhabei Nanshi. The second phase is the municipal schools in other districts of the city. The second phase is all municipal and private schools in the various districts of the city. The first phase of work is currently underway and will last until the end of this year. The second phase of work will be scheduled to begin depending on the results of the first phase.

Clinics Established The work currently underway includes the establishment of two clinics. The Zhabei District is located in Yinan Elementary School, and the Nanshi District is located in Wanzhu Elementary School. All medicines are supplied by the Health Bureau. If students in the schools in these two districts are sick, they can be sent to the above two clinics for treatment. However, because there are many schools, it is hoped that more clinics can be added in the short term to meet the needs. As for the physical examination of students in the various schools, it is also currently underway.

Special Clinics In addition to the above-mentioned clinics, there is also a dental clinic attached to the Municipal Education Bureau, which hires specialist dentists to treat dental diseases. There is also a scrofulous eye clinic, which is currently being planned and hopefully established in the short term. In addition to setting up clinics, training courses are also organized in the three districts. The Zhabei District is located in He'an Elementary School, the Nanshi District is located in the auditorium of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and the Gaoyang District is located in Gaoyang Elementary School. The municipal schools in the various districts must send three teachers and staff to attend lectures. The Health Bureau will send people to guide and lecture on common hygiene knowledge, general physiology, pathology, and first aid methods to make them understand the meaning and importance of hygiene facilities. The training courses are held at night, two hours each day, for a total of 32 hours to be completed. If good influence and effects can be obtained after completion, they will continue to be held and more content will be added.

Special Feature

A Respectful Announcement to All National University and Middle School Students: Implementing Education to Save the Nation ((1) by You Huai-gao 173

(1) Three Major Problems in Saving the Nation

The nation has reached such a dangerous state that I believe there is not a single person who does not want to save it. Because if we do not save it, the nation will perish. When the time of national subjugation arrives, even if you have ardent hearts, I am afraid it will be too late. At the very least, you will have to endure a long period of slavery like the people of India. After being slaves, there will be a stain on our bright history of the Republic of China, which can never be erased. Now that the nation has not yet perished, there is still an opportunity to save it. Therefore, we should immediately decide on the following three problems concerning saving the nation:

First, who should take the lead in taking responsibility for implementing national salvation?

Second, how should we save the nation?

Third, how do we determine a common period and goal for saving the nation?

The people of China are said to number 400 million. In reality, it is impossible for all the people to participate in saving the nation. If we examine the people from the political, academic, agricultural, industrial, and commercial circles, we will realize that university and middle school students in the academic world, in terms of their status, responsibility, and value, should take the lead in taking responsibility for saving the nation. Therefore, I will first explain the status, responsibility, and value of university and middle school students, which will make it clear.

(2) The Status of University and Middle School Students

The government is currently unable to save the nation on its own because it cannot solve the four major issues of finance, military affairs, foreign affairs, and transportation. As a result, it cannot solve the four major issues of education, agriculture, industry, and commerce for the people. Although they know that without real industry, we cannot survive, and without education, we cannot establish the nation, they are genuinely in a position of being willing but unable to do so because they are busy with their own affairs. Understanding this principle means we do not need to rely entirely on the government, nor do we need to blame the government. Then, what should we do? We should request the government to advocate for things we are capable of doing and are confident in, and then, under the supervision of the government, we can build our future.

Looking at the farmers across the country, they have physical strength but lack intellect, they have conscience but lack practical strength, and they possess the virtues of diligence and thrift, but they lack the ability to strive forward. Before receiving education, they cannot participate in saving the nation. Looking at the workers across the country, they share the same fate as the farmers and are busy seeking survival and making a living, leaving them no time to participate in saving the nation. Looking at the merchants across the country, along with the most influential new bankers and new industrialists, they are all huddled in several treaty ports, each building their golden towers and silver vaults, and they may not be able to advocate for saving the nation.

If the government cannot save the nation, and the farmers, workers, and merchants do not come forward to save the nation, then who will take on this heavy and arduous task of saving the nation? After thinking it over, I can only ask the university and middle school students across the country to initiate this work of saving the nation.

Fellow students, you are the people in the country who have received higher education, who are known for loving the country and having passionate blood, you are people with healthy bodies and clear minds, you are people with relatively concrete plans, and you are the one out of every ten thousand people who can be leaders. Therefore, I believe that those who have received education above the high school level are the ones who bear the heavy responsibility of saving the nation. If you still do not come forward to save the nation, you will be as incapable as the government and the ignorant people. In the future, there is no need to scold the government, because scolding the government is scolding yourself. In the future, there is no need to laugh at others, because laughing at others is laughing at yourself. If you are not willing to take responsibility for saving the nation, China will undoubtedly perish. Therefore, I hope that you students will create some earth-shattering achievements. Although you are currently living in a dark society, under conservative families and corrupt governments, the frustration and depression in your hearts are greater than anyone else's, but you must never lose heart and fall into the path of self-destruction and debauchery. Because suicide and debauchery are mostly unavoidable social pathologies in times of extreme depression, but ultimately, you must strive for the future and take responsibility for improvement in order to maintain the true character of young patriots. Now that we have explained your position in saving the nation, let us talk about your responsibilities.

(3) The Responsibilities of University and Middle School Students

We have extremely vast land, but it is full of bandits, so developing agriculture is your responsibility. We have an extremely large population, but most of them are ignorant, so running education is your responsibility. We have inexhaustible treasures, but they are buried deep underground, so mining is your responsibility. We have thousands of years of civilization and history, but everything is backward, so promoting science is your responsibility. We have the oppression of strong neighbors, but no one can resist it, so improving military affairs is your responsibility. We have economic aggression and cannot save ourselves, so creating industries is your responsibility. This is not just empty talk that can be dismissed; we must gather countless agriculturalists, educators, engineers, scientists, military experts, and industrialists to work together wholeheartedly to succeed. You are all specialized talents, and you placed this responsibility on yourselves early on during your studies. Therefore, you will have to take on this responsibility sooner or later. However, the prerequisite issue is the entire education problem. Currently, there are countless specialized talents with true knowledge and practical skills who cannot get a corresponding position after graduating and develop their talents because the majority of the people are uneducated. The interior cannot thrive without education, and without the interior thriving, there are no great undertakings to be done. Without undertakings, there is no need for talents, so thousands upon thousands of highly educated talents gather in the metropolis, creating a situation where there are more people than jobs, leading to the tragic situation where people are not used for what they are good at, and what they are used for is not what they studied. Therefore, only the work of saving the nation through education can genuinely create countless opportunities and outlets for talents. This is your significant responsibility.

Recent News from the Shanghai Women's Supplementary School 179

The Shanghai Women's Supplementary School on Hualong Road, founded by Zhou Zhensao, plans to expand its scope starting next semester, dividing it into three departments: general, vocational, and home economics. Furthermore, the school's existing buildings are insufficient for use. The school is currently seeking suitable housing to be used specifically as dormitories, home economics classrooms, and practice rooms. The tuition fees charged by the school are already low, but to help adult women who have dropped out of school, it is planned to further reduce them to promote widespread education.

A Scene from the Fierce Battle of Jiangda Football: Jinan Wins Fudan by a Score of 4-0

Luo Haiguang Scores Three Goals Alone; Excellent Sportsmanship on Both Sides 186

In the Jiangnan Eight University Football Championship, in the number of circular, I reach military-like meeting period, Jinan and Fudan meet with unbeaten records, with the ambition to resolve the championship. The only remaining opponent for both sides is Jiaotong University. They will face Jiaotong University again tomorrow. The referees yesterday were Wang and Fudan. The lineups of both sides are as follows:

Jinan University

Yun Feng           Wang Nanzhen

Lai Zuorong                    Chen Zhenxiang

Deng Hanjie (Up)    Liu Zukan

Fudan University

Gong Yixun (Up)
