Feng Nianhan                    Zhou Shaowen

Li Lin

(One Defender, One Attacker) Surrounded by Three to Four Thousand Fans, the Battle Begins. Jinan Immediately Issues a General Attack Order, But Repeated Advances Are Repeatedly Blocked. Guan Xunan Guards the Back, Looking Left and Right, Spares No Effort. Yang Mingjin Also Carefully Guards the Goal. After Twenty Minutes of Jinan's Fierce Attack, They Achieve Nothing and Gradually Show Signs of Slackness. Fudan Takes This Opportunity to Start Pushing Forward, Approaching Jinan's Goal, But Either They Are Too Slow to Kick the Ball, or They Shoot Without Aim, and Their Efforts Are in Vain. In This Half Hour, One Attack and One Defense, One Advance and One Retreat, They Achieve Nothing. Luo Haiguang Is Determined and Repeatedly Shoots at the Goal from a Distance. At This Point, There Is a New Development.

(Haiguang Scores Continuously) The Stuffy Situation Is Broken Only in the Last Ten Minutes of the First Half. Yun Feng Passes the Ball Across the Field, and Liu Zukan Gets It and Advances Straight. The Defender Rushes Over. Liu Does Not Wait for Him to Arrive and Sends It to the Front of the Goal. Zhang Hongzao Charges Straight Alone. Guan Xunan Blocks, But Zhang Falls Before He Can Shoot. Yang Mingjin Is Too Close. Haiguang Shoots from the Gap in the Crowd and Scores. Jinan Opens the Scoring with a Score of 1-0. Although Fudan Kicks Off Again to Attack, It Is Again Obtained by Jinan. Liu Zukan Advances on the Right Side and Sends It Diagonally. Wang Nanzhen Responds on the Left Wing. Guan Xunan Flies Out. Liang Shutang Intercepts and Shoots from a Distance, Hitting the Top of the Goal and Bouncing Back. Zhang Hongzao Tries to Attack Again, But He Is Blocked by Guan. Pan Haiguang Comes Up and Pushes It In. Three Minutes Later, the First Half Ends. Jinan Wins 2-0.

(Nanzhen Headers the Ball) Fudan Loses Its Fighting Spirit Due to Losing Two Goals in a Row. They Actively Counterattack as Before. The Five Tigers Attack Together, Knocking on the City Gate. Yu Shunzhang Deeply Buries Himself in Heavy Defense. No One Is In Front of Him, and He Can Take It in One Fell Swoop. Who Would Have Thought That He Would Not Shoot at the Empty Goal but Fly It Out of the Woods? What a Pity. At This Time, Jinan's Five Forwards Have Switched Positions with Each Other. Liu Zukan Is in Wang Nanzhen's Position, Chen Zhenxiang Is Transferred Outward, Zhang Hongzao Pads Chen's Position, and Wang Nanzhen Is in Liu's Position. Zhang Hongzao Is Sometimes on the Right Wing, Circling a Few Times, and Wang Nanzhen Takes a Step Without Stopping and Heads the Ball into the Net. Only Five Minutes Have Passed Since the Start of the Second Half.

(Another One Comes) With Three Goals in a Row, Fudan Is Still Determined to Break Through the Opponent's Goal. They Have Opportunities, But They Lose to Luck and Their Own Feet. Lin Bingcheng Fiercely Attacks the Goal, As Fast as an Arrow, But Unfortunately, He Misses by Two Inches and Hits the Top of the Goal and Bounces Down. Yu Shunzhang Sends the Ball Diagonally from the Right Direction, But No One Is in Front of the Goal, and No One Receives It, Letting It Slip Away. What a Pity. Luo Haiguang Then Comes on to Refuel. Sure Enough, Another One Comes. Jinan Scores Its Fourth Goal and the Game Ends.

(Everyone Is Harmonious) Yesterday, the Sportsmanship on Both Sides Was Excellent, and They Were Extremely Harmonious. The Losers Still Strove to Win Despite Losing, and the Winners Still Did Not Relax Despite Winning. The Fighting Spirit Is Commendable. We Sincerely Hope to Maintain It for a Long Time. The Failure of Fudan Is Blamed on Something. The Action Is Slightly Slow, and They Missed Many Opportunities. The Defenders, However, Are Strong and Worthy of Praise. It Is Only Natural That the Excellent Ones Win, and Fudan Is Also Willing to Submit.

Second Day of the Second Round of the Public Exhibition Cup International Handball: China Loses Again 194

Western Team 3 Points, Chinese Team 1 Point

The first Public Exhibition Cup International Handball Tournament held its second day of the second round yesterday afternoon at 6 PM at the Xiqing venue. In the second singles match, Sun Ke and the opposing player each won a game first, showing equal strength and fierce competition that was rarely seen. Unfortunately, in the third game, Sun was physically weak and lacked stamina, resulting in a loss. The fifth and eighth matches were also lost successively, while Lu fought hard and won the seventh match, creating a situation of China 1, Western 3. The only hope for our Chinese team lies in winning all the doubles matches today. Although the task is difficult, it is not entirely impossible.

Fujian Traders Continue to Purchase Hakka Xiang Rice 207

| Feng Hu Stops Purchasing and Switches to Lower River Rice |

Yesterday, the Hakka Xiang rice market situation showed that Fujian province had a strong appetite, and the market slightly turned around. High-grade glutinous and non-glutinous Xiang rice each gradually approached one cent. Medium and lower grades were stable. The entire market opened with around 2,000 bags. Among them, besides the Quanzhou traders purchasing 400 bags, all were purchased by 漳州 traders. The Northern traders and hoarders had no appetite. The Northern traders said that because rice prices in that area were falling, transportation and sales were not worthwhile. Even the usually popular Clear Water Bo Dao rice has recently fallen to around 11 yuan. When calculated with the Shanghai market price, it is also not profitable. Therefore, although Su rice has the possibility of transshipment, its appetite cannot be smooth. Yesterday, all types of rice from the Lower River fell. Hoarders took the opportunity to buy, so they did not pay attention to Hakka Xiang rice. Hakka Xiang rice had a small improvement due to sufficient inventory. Fortunately, the arrival of new supplies has not been strong recently, and the Fujian traders' buying appetite is still strong, so the market has managed to stabilize. The entire day saw purchases of 1,000 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice at prices of 8.50 to 8.34 yuan, 150 bags of 砶 early rice at a price of 6.5 yuan, 250 bags of Wuhu machine-milled rice at prices of 9.75 to 9.65 yuan, and 525 bags of Hunan machine-milled oil rice at prices of 8.80 to 8.67 yuan.

Yesterday, as foreign exchange rates tightened frequently, the settlement price for hardware imports increased significantly. This is because the foreign exchange rate is tight and prices are high, while Shanghai's prices are low and inventory is shallow. If actual transactions start, the supply and demand will not meet, and a surge in prices can be expected.

Coal: Kailuan Lump Coal Prices Increase Covertly 214

Major Traders Hoarding for Speculation

Small Retailers Suffer Significant Losses

Kailuan lump coal, previously due to 峰煤 銷 sales, the company reduced prices for bargain sales, selling for only 6.5 taels per ton. Recently, the market's spot supply is moving, and it feels lacking. Ordinary peer retailers find it quite difficult to purchase it for a time. The reason is that the company's arrivals are all pre-ordered by major traders who are hoarding it for speculation. Therefore, the selling price has secretly increased. The market's quoted prices yesterday were still at 6.5 taels from the company, but there were no goods available for transaction. However, the major traders were selling for over 7 taels per ton. According to observations by ordinary people, prices are expected to rise further during the Lunar New Year.

Page 17

Free Talk

Budding (1) 239

— Heng

From that day on, Little A Mao refused to step into the high-walled house with the courtyard ever again.

He was only twelve years old this year and had a father who used to be a copper craftsman and was now a zinc craftsman. His father had a nose that was reddened by alcohol; his own nose was red for three seasons of the year because he didn’t have enough clothes. Not only red, but also constantly running. As for his mother, he had no recollection of her in his small memory. Simply put, there were only two of them: father and son, son and father. The two ate together and slept together.

And the father, as usual, had the temper of a man who loved to drink. During the day, he would make his son do things that almost only an adult could do. In his mind, Little A Mao had been snotty for more than ten years, which was not a small amount; if he really couldn't do it, a mouth would help him do it. At night, he would spread himself out like a clumsy ox, squeezing the little one into a corner, unable to sleep and unable to move; as soon as the sky turned white, he would kick him out of the sweaty, alcohol-smelling quilt, so that he could sleep comfortably by himself until broad daylight.

For all of this, Little A Mao never resisted, and no matter how much he was beaten or scolded, he never cried.

The two of them lived like this, in the most dilapidated room in a broken alley, stealthily, monotonously, and solitarily, as if they had been forgotten by all of mankind.

But some usual families would always think of the copper craftsman A Fa whenever they needed to install a skylight or repair a roof.

On such days, we would see Little A Mao carrying a long iron tube on his back, which was not much smaller than his own body, following his father, who had his hands free, taking three steps and running two steps into those high-walled houses. He watched his father work, handing him the hammer and the scissors. When he didn't need to hand him the scissors or the hammer, he stood there blankly, looking at this and looking at that.

But his eyes were sharp, sharp and deep.

That day was the same. It was cold that day, and he was only wearing a thin cotton jacket and pants. He squatted by the stove that his father used for work like a cat warming itself by the stove, his face and sleeves covered in snot. He was waiting for his father's command, and the knuckle-rapping that often came with it. "Add charcoal!" the command came.

Little A Mao was afraid of being too slow, and quickly grabbed a large pair of fire tongs with his small hands.

Now, that family had a girl who was about ten years old. In his haste to grab the fire tongs, Little A Mao inadvertently touched the edge of her clothes with his sleeve. The girl quickly pulled back, looked at him, and with a feminine gesture, took out a handkerchief and wiped her clothes for a long time.

"Filthy, so disgusting!" As if talking to herself.

He wanted to answer, "Who told you to walk over here?" But with his father there, he didn't dare to do so.

He just stared at her with deep eyes.

That girl was naturally very clean, her hair was slicked back, and her face was covered in powder and rouge, just like a fashionable young woman. Like a little goblin, Little A Mao thought in his heart; he remembered that his father often called the women who dressed extravagantly goblins. But he just thought it, his anger still couldn't subside. "Your mom is..." He thought even more maliciously, but the anger was still the same.

A Fa climbed onto the roof.

"Pump the bellows," he shouted from above.

Little A Mao huffed and puffed as he pumped the bellows below. While pumping, he was paying attention. At first, he pumped very slowly, but when the "little goblin" came closer, he pushed hard inside.

"Damn it!" The other one cursed like a ghost.

Seeing the "little goblin" covered in ash, he felt comfortable in his heart; "You came up to me yourself," he said victoriously.

"This place is ours, not yours, can't I come here!"

"We're working."

"Little devil, if you're working, you'll be king!"

Hearing that "little devil," Little A Mao immediately widened his eyes and stopped pumping the bellows; if that girl hadn't quickly been called inside, no one could have guessed how he would have responded.

Civilized Weapon 240

— Ye Shengtao

In the past, when shops had "special sales" or "anniversaries," they would hire a few military bands (the character for "band" was usually pronounced like the "le" in "happy") to blow and beat their instruments, in order to attract the attention of passersby. Now, this method seems to have been eliminated. Only on remote small streets, there are occasionally a few outdated small shops that send out a combination of trumpets and flutes, playing the tune "Drizzling Rain" or "Sister, I Love You." Passersby know what's going on and walk by without turning their heads. This lonely music is only listened to lonely by the cloth shop under the eaves.

Now, Shanghai shops have another way to attract attention. Even if it's not a "special sale" or an "anniversary," they also install a radio under the eaves in front of the door. Fortunately, there are so many broadcasting stations that they can receive sound continuously from early morning to late at night, so they keep the machine on all the time. Thus, the space, which is already filled with the sound of trams and cars, is mixed with the "ballad" of the three-stringed instrument, the scabby voice of "crying for Miao Gengdu's grandfather," and the old gun's throat singing "Drizzling Rain" and "Sister, I Love You," and so on.

But this method may not really attract attention. Only when it was first popular, a few passersby stood in front of the shops with radios, staring blankly. Later, just like hiring a few military bands to blow and beat their instruments, you can "ballad":: "Sister, I Love You," passersby still walk their own way. Looking at the shop assistants in the store, it seems that none of them are listening to these "old tunes every day." So, who exactly is the radio receiving sound for? This is probably only known by the shop sign. However, the number of newly installed radios is still increasing, as if it would be a disgrace to a big store not to have a radio.

There is a radio in my left neighbor's house, and the sound is clear and loud, so the quality is probably not bad. But their way of dealing with this fellow is too wonderful. They are always turning the dial there, the old man sang half a sentence, then came a woman's ditty, the ditty didn't finish a song, then came a high-pitched Western throat::: What do they want to listen to, I haven't figured it out in three or four months. Maybe their interest lies in turning that dial. Otherwise, it's just that they "have" a radio丨a radio is fashionable, people all "have" it, so they must "have" it too.

I also heard that many opium addicts in Shanghai are too lazy to go out, so they use the radio to communicate with each other. A few people set up their own broadcasting stations, and at one or two o'clock at night, they broadcast from the opium bed: "Zhang Lao San, have you had dinner yet? Li Lao Si, you're in the mahjong game tomorrow night, don't get up too late." Ah, modern civilized life丨

Saying "radio saves the country" (Mr. Wu Zhihui's talk about "motor saves the country" was published in yesterday's newspaper, and this style of mine has a source,) is of course almost absurd and unbelievable. However, if this radio guy can be used well, for example, to unite the will of the masses, impart true knowledge, and report accurate news:::: Then, from a social point of view, its value is indeed amazing. Conversely, if it only becomes a substitute for the "street military band," only becomes an ornament for shops and homes, only becomes a communication machine for opium addicts, and the only things transmitted are "who's grandfather is crying" and "who's mother is crying," then I ask, why should society value such "ingenious and lewd" gadgets?

The value of all so-called "civilized weapons" does not exist in themselves, but in their impact on society. This can be viewed from two aspects: first, who is holding it in their hands, and second, how is it being used. Take motors, for example. The United States can be considered a country with a lot of motors, but there are large groups of hungry people on the avenues of the cities, playing the march of hunger. This is because all the motors are held in the hands of capitalism. If those motors also had a share for the hungry, the hungry would no longer be hungry. At that time, the value of motors would be more than just "saving the country"? Another example is airplanes. In recent years, the Soviet Union has used them to spread seeds and kill pests. This has expanded mankind's ability to overcome nature, and the value of airplanes is so noble. But when they are used as bombers and reconnaissance planes, who, except for the ambitious people who are haggling over the military reduction conference, still recognizes their value?

New Women 丨Actors of Love 241

— Jianquan

The best virtues of women are love and children. Only with these two things can they express their truth and greatness. However, the new women, the "flowers of society" of today, are not enough to talk about love, and they are not willing to have children, thinking that it is a misfortune and a burden: really, they are just "monsters."

Although they are not enough to talk about love, they love to talk about love; although they love to talk about love, they do not want to get the exclusive love of a man, nor do they want to get a kind of happiness in lust; they just want to win the admiration, respect, worship, and surrounding of the men they have won over. In short, they only need some men who are as gentle as a kitten to be love slaves in front of them.

When they want to get the love of a certain man, in other words, when they want to seduce him to be a love slave, they also know that there is no success without hard work; but when they succeed, they only put him in the ranks of slaves, higher or lower. Their love for him is just like a master loving a loyal dog.

They cannot love any one person exclusively; because their emotions are indefinite, their souls are restless, their hearts seem to be a bottomless black hole, and their tastes and understanding are very lacking: so their intellectual knowledge is very dark. If we try in vain to tempt them, wanting to get their hearts, souls, intelligence, and special qualities, and to be treated differently, as women of ancient times were overwhelmed by the value and enthusiasm of a man, then it is simply as impossible as a prisoner picking up his fist and trying to open an iron door. They have a kind of theoretical skill, and they know a little about the general psychology of mankind, especially the psychology of men. They can manage their lovers according to their shortcomings and according to their character; at the same time, they have some unexpected kindness, subtle care, and infinite tenderness to give to their love prisoners. They are intuitive and inspired; they often use a cat-like spirit to see from the eyes of their lovers that kind of gentle beggar-like plea, and the fear of the defeated, and the trembling of willingly being conquered, without him having to express it with his lips, they already fully understand that he is already intoxicated. Their love of decoration, rather than being for their own sake, is more for winning the love of men, and they will also put on a kind of child's attitude: because they themselves consider that only in this way can they be more seductive and can they win the offerings of men of favor. Their fondness for the new and dislike of the old is very alarming. In a person, everything that initially made her happy, made her excited, made her restless, made her emotional, and made her worried, soon became ordinary, vulgar, and tasteless.

In short, the new women, the social flowers of today, are all actors, actors of love, re-enacting a play, just acting as usual: they have no love. For these actors, one can only also play a role like them and deal with them. Whoever is infatuated with them is blind!

Random Musings 242

— Ye Lingfeng

Three Isabellas

For the past ten years, I've been immersed in the dreams that every young person indulges in, experiencing the world's pessimism, separations, and reunions. This has made me cherish and love my books even more. I feel that in times of joy, they can be neglected without jealousy, and in my loneliness, they can console me without dwelling on the past.

At the same time, only they truly understand how arduous and perilous the journey of a young, contemplative soul is within the kingdom of the heart.

Therefore, I cherish each of my books, for they are my most loyal companions, willing to sacrifice themselves for me.

Five years ago, I received a letter from a woman named Qin, trapped under the yoke of her family. She lamented that her heartless elder brother had stripped her of all freedom and was about to sell her life's happiness. She asked for my help one last time. I knew what she hoped for, but I was unwilling to give alms lightly. So, I made my silent companion make a self-sacrificing sacrifice.

It was a collection of poems by the short-lived English poet John Keats. I knew it contained a similarly poignant story, telling of a young woman named Isabella, whose lover was murdered by her cruel brothers. Upon discovering the news, she stole her lover's head, buried it in a pot of basil, placed it in her bedroom, and secretly watered her never-ending love with tears every day.

I sent the book to her, with a short note attached:

"Cherish it. When necessary, it can replace a person's head."

Needless to say, I lost the book forever, until this day. But I do not regret it, because I know it has long fulfilled the mission I entrusted to it.

December 20th

Childhood Dreams 243

— Gao Ming

Recently, a magazine requested dreams for its New Year's issue and sent me a request form. Until now, I have not only failed to send them a dream, but I haven't even had one. The postage stamp on the request form has been used up by me. Thinking about it, I feel terribly sorry.

Even I find it hard to believe that at my age, when I should be dreaming the most, the period of dreaming has long vanished, I don't know where. Only childhood dreams remain, leaving faint traces in my memory.

When I was little, my dreams were so sweet. My first ambition was to become a diplomat, hoping to use my personal talent to make China the world's leading power through diplomacy. Because at that time, I thought that a country's reputation came entirely from diplomacy. Later, even I knew this idea was unreliable, so I changed my ambition to become a military engineering expert. In middle school, I devoted myself to this. My physics, chemistry, and mathematics were always ranked first in the class. Later, due to family reasons, this ambition could not be realized either. If I had to say it was a regret, it could be considered a regret.

In terms of personal life, my dreams were even more elaborate. I dreamed of being a wealthy man in the future, with a house as big as a racetrack, with cars, small trains, motorized bicycles, bicycles, horses, and sports facilities like football fields, basketball courts, and swimming pools. Every day, I would get up and go to bed on time, managing the whole family with foreign orders. I would never marry, just play with my family...

Vanished, the period of dreaming has vanished. Besides painful memories, what else does it give me? In terms of current reality, nothing matches my dreams at the time. Only the point of not marrying has, after many twists and turns, become a reality. Is this the only thing worth consoling myself with?

Full-Length Fiction

The Crossroads of Times and Love, Part 23 245

— Zhang Ziping

"I'm sorry." Shi Guang's empty hand emerged from his suit pocket again.

Pastor Habar's residence was right behind the church. In terms of area, it was more than three times the size of the church itself, a two-story Western-style house, with a garden spanning more than one mu in front.

Upon reaching Pastor Habar's porch, Cao Shiguang removed his coat and felt hat, and Haiquan also took off his hat and untied his scarf. A doorman took them and hung them on a coat rack. Haiquan followed Shiguang straight into Pastor Habar's living room. Many guests had already arrived, some white, some yellow, some men, some women. Cao Shiguang pointed to a white man in his fifties and told Haiquan:

"That is Pastor Habar."

After Shiguang said this, he walked over and nodded to the old foreigner.

"Mr. Habar, let me introduce a friend to you, he is also a sincere seeker of the Way..." Shiguang said, pulling Haiquan's hand and introducing him to Habar. Habar's face quickly filled with a smile, and he came over to shake hands with Haiquan.

"Very good, very good. What is your surname, sir?"

Shiguang quickly answered Habar for Haiquan.

"I'm a little busy right now, Mr. Cao, please entertain Mr. Lin for me."

Habar said, shaking Haiquan's hand again, saying "I'm sorry" twice, then went to talk to that white man.

"Let's go to the auditorium and take a look, shall we? See if those beautiful goods have arrived yet."

Seeing Habar so busy, so alert and active, without a trace of sincerity, Haiquan was a little disappointed. But having already come, he had no choice but to follow Shiguang to the large auditorium in front. It was past four o'clock, but the believers who had arrived were still as scarce as morning stars, and there were no beautiful goods to be seen. Haiquan then questioned Shiguang, "It's still early, isn't it? They haven't arrived yet."

But Haiquan always felt that coming with Shiguang was a mistake.

"Please wait a moment, let me go ask old Habar if there's anything to be done today. If not, after the prayer meeting, shall we go out and have some fun?"

Haiquan thought that his time was worthless anyway, and only nodded.

Shiguang left and didn't return for a long time. Haiquan occupied a seat in the middle row and read a New Testament. But he paid close attention to everyone who came in from outside, and after looking, he speculated about what kind of people they were. As Shiguang said, later, several women of somewhat questionable character arrived in twos and threes. Whenever he saw a woman being followed in by a man, he found that woman particularly annoying, even if she was a beauty.

The bell rang. A large group of believers poured in from outside. Finally, he saw Cao Shiguang accompanying a man in his forties, wearing a very simple blue cotton robe, walking in while talking. The way Shiguang treated him was very intimate and sincere, and the old gentleman just nodded frequently.

"So, according to my idea, it must be done this way..."

Supplement to the Shanghai News

Comments

To Future Parents 246

— Nong Zhe

The responsibilities of current parents are certainly great, but the responsibilities of future parents are even greater. Current parents must do their best to seek happiness for their children, but future parents must plan in advance how to create excellent children in the future.

We have the instinct to develop sexual desire, but we also have the responsibility to preserve the race. A lovely life between the sexes is certainly a right of life, but striving to raise children is our bounden duty. So, when we want to live that sweet life between the sexes, we should first ask ourselves, "Has our concrete plan for raising children been properly prepared?"

The first question is, what is our physical condition like, is it healthy? Originally, a person's hair and skin are inherited from their parents. Our future children are differentiated from our bodies. If our bodies are strong now, our future children will also be healthy. Conversely, if our bodies have defects, our future children will also be unhealthy. Please check for ourselves, what is our physical condition like, is it healthy? Secondly, what is our economic strength like, can we make ends meet?

When we have children, the amount on the budget will be much higher than without. Bearing the responsibility of seeking happiness for children, economic expenditure is difficult to estimate. If there is no more abundant preparation beforehand, how can we bear to make our future children suffer?

Regarding the educational aspect, do we have the patience to educate children day and night? When things don't go our way, will we vent our anger by hitting our children? Will we indulge in pleasure and leave our children to be raised by wet nurses? Will we avoid giving our children bad suggestions? Can we create a good environment for our children? Can we give our children the opportunity to receive appropriate education?

Future parents! Do we already have the above strengths? Only when we have these many strengths can we begin to lead that life between the sexes and become parents. If we don't have them? Then we are simply not qualified to be parents. To put it bluntly, we don't even have the qualifications to marry, unless we have taken birth control pills beforehand.

In addition, subjects such as physiology, eugenics, child psychology, etc., are also of great importance to our future parents for research and implementation.

Future parents, please listen to my words!

If we cannot educate our children well in the future, it is better not to give birth, so as not to increase the number of beggars, petty thieves, and small robbers.

If you don't want to have children, you must not get married, because marriage requires having children.

If you don't want to get married, you must not be human, because being human has the responsibility of preserving the race.

Future parents! Please do not think that my words are extreme. In the time between this "present" and the "future," observe, study, and explore the way of parents!

Mud Winter Bamboo Shoots 247

— Yi Yi Guan Zhu

It is now winter, and winter bamboo shoots are on the market. Friends who are particular about food must eat winter bamboo shoots this winter. Whether it's "winter bamboo shoots fried with shredded pork" or "winter bamboo shoots fried with vegetable hearts," there are endless uses for winter bamboo shoots. In short, for any delicacy that can use winter bamboo shoots, winter bamboo shoots are always used.

Indeed, winter bamboo shoots are as delicious as other seasonal delicacies, so the price is not very cheap either.

However, in the Sixteen Paved Street area of ​​Nanshi, there are some petty hooligans who pick up bundles of winter bamboo shoots in their hands, each bundle containing about five or six, and peddle them along the road for only two dimes. They are cheap, of course, but who knows that when each one is peeled open, it is a package of mud! The good ones even have cockle and clam shells mixed in. Naturally, they are extra fresh.

Alas! Don't laugh. I think if these "mud winter bamboo shoots" are bought for your own consumption, then don't say anything about it. It's like doing a good deed for two dimes, helping a petty hooligan. If they are bought to give as gifts, then it's really a big joke! Moreover, the giver doesn't realize that there is a package of mud inside. But the receiver will suspect that you are deliberately making fun of them.

Alas! In short, the term "mud winter bamboo shoots" is both novel and unique. I think it is something that the readers have never heard or seen before? So I am specially revealing it here.

Science

Production of Saccharin 248

— Xing

Saccharin is an organic compound, whose chemical formula

is C6H4COSO2NH. The starting point for manufacturing saccharin is Toluene, and the procedure can be divided into three steps.

(1) Sulfonation: First, mix toluene with concentrated sulfuric acid of equal weight. Place it on a double boiler and warm it gently until a drop of this mixture can completely dissolve in water. This usually takes about 30 minutes. After the reaction is complete (that is, it can dissolve), let it cool and slowly pour it into cold water. The resulting o-toluenesulfonic acid dissolves in water. The reaction is as follows:

C6H6CH3 + H2SO4 ∈ C6H4

CH3SO3H + H2O

Then add charcoal acid (or calcium carbonate) and boil it. Then the excess sulfuric acid is converted into barium sulfate (or calcium) and precipitates, which is removed by filtration. The filtrate is toluenesulfonic acid barium (or calcium). Slowly add dilute sulfuric acid to liberate the organic acid, adding it until no more white precipitate is produced. And filter.

(2) Oxidation: The filtrate contains o-toluenesulfonic acid, at this time add an appropriate amount of potassium permanganate as an oxidizing agent. Apply a little temperature, and you will get benzoic acid o-sulfonic acid. The reaction is as follows:

C6H4CH3SO3H + 3O = C6H4

COSHSO3H + H2O

(3) Saccharin substitution: At this time, pass in ammonia gas, or add ammonia water. Let stand for several hours to obtain.

NH3 C6H4CONH 2H2O

SO3H NH3 C6H4SO2NH 2H2O

This substance is not easily soluble in water, so its sodium salt is usually used. The above solution can be added with sodium carbonate, stirring frequently to help the emission of carbonic acid gas. After filtration, evaporate and concentrate the filtrate, and saccharin will crystallize out after cooling. Collect it and dry it in a desiccator to obtain it.

The taste of saccharin is 400 times sweeter than ordinary sucrose. Hence it is called saccharin. One part of saccharin dissolved in 50,000 parts of water is still very sweet. The use of saccharin is as a sugar substitute, but because sugar cannot be used due to pathological reasons, saccharin is used to provide sweetness. Such as for people with diabetes, kidney disease, etc. But ordinary merchants often seek profit and use it in sugary foods and cakes. This substance is not beneficial to the human body and should not be eaten in large quantities.

The Organization of Three Kinds of Groups 249

Dear Editor:

Since your newspaper established a circulating library in the Mainland business district, the established lending methods allow us to sit in the store all day and still have plenty of opportunities to read. But books are as vast as the sea, how should many of our semi-literate friends choose which books to borrow? Once we get a book, what is the best way to read it? If we encounter difficult places, who should we ask for guidance? Therefore, even though your newspaper has designed everything meticulously, we still have a feeling of "sighing at the door of the library."

I believe that we young people, in this time of national crisis, should each strive to study diligently to save the dangerous situation. Although there is no shortage of diligent people, they are like a pile of scattered sand, lacking proper unity. Individual knowledge is extremely limited, and pondering alone is twice the effort with half the result. Difficulties and obstacles are rarely avoided. Colleagues, aware of this, have gathered a few male and female comrades, planning to use their spare time on Sundays to organize a Sunday academic discussion group, dedicated to exchanging knowledge and encouraging each other. If there are colleagues who agree with our opinions, why not join us! Zhang Siwei, et al.

(1) One of the most common phenomena in many groups in our country is that they are full of vitality at the beginning. Otherwise, like fireflies passing by, what is the point?

If you go the other way, you will not have time to compete for positions and seek advantages, how can you promote the meeting and how can you transform life?

Especially saving money, saving time, and saving space, it is more suitable for the environment of ordinary shop employees.

The Social Escape Artists 250

— Tianfang

Near where I live, there is an ancient temple inhabited by several ascetic monks. Every morning, the rhythmic sound of their wooden fish, "ge ge," carries to my pillow, often filling me with compassionate emotions as I imagine their lives. These pitiful selfish individuals have fallen completely for the Indian charade, filled with the desire for ascension to immortality and Buddhahood, yet still burdened with a decaying body that requires the sustenance of the human world. In the end, with eyes closed, they are returned to the yellow earth. As for becoming immortal or a Buddha, let others name it. Isn't the end of life the same as for ordinary people? What is the difference between "studying Buddhism" and "waiting to die?" If they speak of praying for rebirth in the Western Paradise, but knew that the "Heavenly Abode" they seek is the homeland of the red-headed Indians, then surely they would not wish to be born in India as descendants of a subjugated people.

Setting everything aside, and regardless of the existence or non-existence of "immortals" and "Buddhas," even if their "ascension in broad daylight," "eternal liberation," and "abiding existence" are not absurd stories, from the process of "birth" to "eternal liberation," "becoming a celestial being," from "mortal" to "immortal" or "Buddha," they cannot but require the sustenance of the human world. Waiting until "merit is perfected" and they ascend to immortality or Buddhahood, they recognize neither parents nor relatives, let alone the farmers and laborers who provide my food and clothing, or the teachers and friends who educate me. Isn't this what is called "each cultivates, each gains?" Are they not the greatest escape artists in society? Fortunately, my Buddha is not so effective that everyone is fooled. So today, the "human" race is still diverse, with no worry about food and clothing, and the world has not been occupied by wild beasts. Otherwise, would the term "human" not have long been extinct? It has been over two thousand years since the birth of my Buddha.

I write this to advise those who tread on the earth but whose souls fly to the heavens.

Film Special Issue

The Republic of China, Year 21, December 23rd, Week (No Additional Cost)

Reader Opinions

"The Continuous Viewing System" 251

— Sen

One who agrees with the abolition of "enter anytime, see the whole film" means that you only need to buy a ticket once and can sit in the theater and watch several screenings of the film. That is, you can "watch continuously."

How exactly did this "continuous viewing system" arise? What kind of impact does it have on theaters and audiences? Should this issue exist? The author wants to discuss it here.

First, let's talk about the reason for the rise of this "continuous viewing system." In simple terms, it is probably because the theater business was not good, and many viewers of such theaters did not arrive on time, so the theater came up with this method. This method is no different for most people, but a few people do find it beneficial to watch more, and are willing to spend money to buy tickets and sit even when they are unwilling to watch the film.

After this system was implemented, both inside and outside the theater became uneasy. For the audience, some people enter after the screening has started, walking into the dark room from the bright outside, unable to see anything, like blind people groping their way. Although there are flashlights to illuminate the way, it is still inconvenient. This, in addition to obstructing the audience's view, also gives the audience a dazzling glare from the flashlight.

Should this issue exist, or should it be abolished? I think readers who see this will definitely agree and say: "It should be abolished."

Here, we must first ask about the purpose of watching movies. To sum it up, there are only two purposes for watching movies: one is for entertainment, and the other is for appreciation. However, under these two purposes, people must be calm and have a fixed time to watch in order to achieve them. When it comes to appreciation, a peaceful state and a quiet environment are even more necessary. But these things cannot be achieved in theaters with "continuous viewing."

In addition, continuous viewing can have extremely bad effects. That is, people can develop the bad habit of not being punctual and can cultivate disorganized behavior. Moreover, many idle people spend their precious time in the theater, which is a great loss for the audience!

Therefore, we must abolish this "continuous viewing" system!

Editor's Note: The continuous viewing system is very common in foreign metropolises and has been in place for more than ten years. In Shanghai, it seems to have only been around for two or three years. This system is especially popular in commercial ports with complex lives, especially for passing travelers. At least it can adapt to a special environment, so abolishing it is really a "problem."

Film Reviews

A Lady from a Humble Home 252

— Xin

A refined lady from a famous family is called a "thousand gold;" a beautiful jade from a humble home is called a "wild girl." It is strange indeed to call a lady from a humble home a "thousand gold."

The plot of this film is intricate and can be praised as a masterpiece. It tells the story of a village girl who is both talented and beautiful, and is beloved by the villagers. However, none of those villagers suit the girl's fancy. At this time, a nobleman comes to the village and commits violence against the good woman. Although the deed is not completed, the woman hates him to the core and declares that she will give herself to whoever can kill the nobleman. Before this, a young man, handsome and outstanding, whose sister had also been humiliated by the nobleman, followed the nobleman and finally killed him with a pistol. The village, considering the murder a major crime, intensified the search, and the young man was captured. As he was about to be executed, the young man took the opportunity to escape. In the middle of the night, the young man came to see the woman, and was chased again. In the end, they eloped to the ends of the earth.

The lighting in the photography is indescribably good, and the editing is unusually novel. From beginning to end, it is connected in a unique format. Watching this film is better than reading a famous book. The director's technique is also commendable. The romance of the first half and the tension of the second half both give people a supreme sense of beauty. Although the interior scenes are ordinary, the exterior scenes are truly captivating, making one's heart itch and eager to explore the truth. The ending, with its stops and starts, seemingly complete yet incomplete three times, could not be achieved without a nimble hand.

Charles Farrell's style is very different from before. His composure and heroism resemble a wanderer and chivalrous guest. His facial expressions are excellent. This is probably his first time co-starring with Joan Bennett. Joan is exquisite and lively. At first, she is romantic and carefree, and then becomes deeply affectionate. The two scenes of the young man being captured and then meeting her in the middle of the night show her acting skills to perfection. The collaboration between the two complements each other. There is a wonderful combination of red flowers and green leaves. The occasional interjections are all pleasing, and although there is no shortage of dialogue, it never makes people feel bored.

Overall, the entire film focuses on the tightness of the plot and the beautification of art. Therefore, the drama's meaning is not worth mentioning, merely showing cause and effect and the sacredness of love. The film makes every effort to depict rural life. We city dwellers, seeing this natural scenery, cannot help but feel a sense of "returning to a utopian village."

This is a great film, and who would say it is inappropriate to praise it as a masterpiece of Fox Corporation?

The Four-No-Like Foreign Films 253

— Jie

Yesterday I saw in this publication that "the costumes in General Yan's Bitter Tea are completely wrong." I couldn't help but have a lot of thoughts.

Hollywood can be said to have never seen any Chinese people. The directors or costume designers have never been to China. The only materials needed are found in Chinatown.

The Chinese in Chinatown are mostly people who have been trading here for generations, and all their customs and habits are stuck in the old customs of the Qing Dynasty. Therefore, it is really difficult to have an accurate reflection of modern China.

What about the students studying abroad? There are quite a few people, but as soon as they cross the Pacific Ocean, they wear Western clothes and shoes, and become completely Westernized. So where can American film companies find reference materials for Chinese clothing? Therefore, they assume that Chinese civilians wear wide-sleeved robes and braided queues, while fake officials wear embroidered official robes and magnificent hats.

I say that this responsibility should be borne by the students studying abroad. They should try to correct everything nearby. The picture below shows the strange costumes in "General Yan's Bitter Tea."

Famous Works Translated

Screen Face (Continued from Yesterday) 254

— Translated by Dunruo

One morning on the way to the makeup room I met Chai Peiqi, "Well, Mrs. Telijiaersiji, how are you?" he asked. "Very good," she said. Chai Peiqi looked at her carefully and slowly said: "Very good, yes, it looks very good 丨丨," he seemed a little dissatisfied. How jealous people are, Telijiaersiji thought after he left.

She went to the store to buy a pot of flowers, bought a washbasin for Bashu, and bought some sweet potatoes for her son. She went to see her son once a week, he was very happy there, she always laughed when she thought of her son, yes, she often laughed now. She bought some pomade to smooth her hair, she bought a green skirt and a hat, she bought a piece of oilcloth to lay on the table where she and her Bashu drank coffee, Mr. Bashu began to hint that she could be his very good partner:::

In October, the people in the work gradually expressed dissatisfaction with her. They assigned her to do extremely easy work, they asked her to walk across a street, stand under a street pillar, cough and crawl forward, but she didn't do anything right, her back was no longer bent, her eyes were accustomed to strong light, and she would no longer be wet, the instructor tried this scene three times without success, cursing and ordering her to go back. The next time she came wearing a white cloak and a green skirt, which made them even more angry. They put her in artificial dirty and dilapidated decorations, but she was no longer real. They strictly ordered her to always wear the set she wore when she first came, and she couldn't understand them at all.

In November, she didn't have much work. In December, she performed in the crowd scene of "The Despised People." She didn't know what Filip shouted, "Why isn't that woman dressed up?" She was dragged into the makeup room and deeply re-printed the wrinkles she had lost in recent months on her face.

"What's wrong?" Filip asked when he walked into the office and saw an ugly and fat woman looking angry and crying.

"Telijiaersiji has been complaining that we haven't asked her to work for a long time," Chai Peiqi told him.

"I'm just saying," she sobbed, "that gentleman is too unfair, because I can now dress a little better and he doesn't want me anymore. According to your meaning, it seems that a working woman like me shouldn't even eat enough. I can still dress up like you want me to, but, God, you can't always tell me to be hungry and wear rags, besides, everything in the movie is fake, you shouldn't fire me just because I can eat my fill:::

"Not so," Filip said angrily, "you misunderstood, on the screen we need more than performance, we need life, real life, but if you want to live a comfortable life yourself, you are worthless to us."

"Yes," Chai Peiqi said very interestingly, "he is right, Mrs. Telijiaersiji, art is a strict supervisor, you must choose, work hard until you die, don't avoid sorrow, breastfeed your child all night丨丨then we will come to ask you for advice again, do you understand what I mean?"

No, she didn't understand him at all, she thought the people here were all crazy, her stubborn back was bent again, and she staggered away in confusion. (End)

Lianhua Company Will Perform Drama for Free 255

— Yun

After the "September 18th" incident, Lianhua Company organized an anti-Japanese association by its actors and actresses, and the entire company carried out military training. This patriotic spirit is indeed admirable. Recently, the drama group of the Lianhua First Factory's club is preparing to stage a drama to aid the Northeast Volunteer Army. It has been decided to invite Mr. Ying Yunwei, Tian Han, and Ouyang Yuqian as consultants. They are now rehearsing Tolstoy's famous play "Resurrection," with Jin Yan, Zheng Junli, Tang Huaiqiu, Ruan Lingyu, Chen Yanyan, Li Zhuozhuo, and others playing the characters in the play. The venue is borrowed from the Lyceum Theatre. The date has been set for three days around the "January 28th" next year. It is said that the proceeds from the ticket sales will be entirely donated to the Northeast Volunteer Army, which is glorifying the country, and all expenses will be borne by the company. This is truly a righteous act.

A month ago, the "Yihua Film Company" was established, and it is now ready. Its first debut work is set to be "Homeless Women." The shooting has reached four or five thousand feet, and there are many wonderful scenes. The script is purely socialized. The scenes of last year's flood disaster and the war situation in Miaohang, Jiangwan, are being set up in the Wusong area, which is quite busy. It is said that the film will be released at the end of the Lunar New Year.

Recently, Hollywood's most recognized close couple is Guiger Rogers and Mervyn Lekoy. Everyone has been clamoring for a long time, saying that they will get married soon. As expected, they are now engaged, and the engagement is only one day before the "wedding bells" ring in the church!

Film Monographs

The Necessary Work for Those Who Love Themselves 258

— Chen Dabeih

The benefit of practicing expressions in front of a mirror is that you can carefully observe the movement of each muscle on your face and the process of gradually tensing or relaxing your emotions. Most people can carefully observe others. But only a very small number of people can carefully observe themselves. Only saints and philosophers can observe the changes in their hearts. We who study the art of performance can practice and experience in this area, and the results are also very amazing.

Ordinary people often neglect the shape of their facial features. It is very easy for a person to close their eyes and silently think of the appearance of relatives and friends. But it is very difficult to silently think of one's own appearance. Many people can never silently think of their own appearance. Ten people take the same picture. At least eight people feel that they are not well photographed; everyone except themselves is well photographed. What is the reason for this? This is because most people are unwilling to pay too much attention to their own appearance. In fact, most people in society today do not know themselves. They only know how to know others and never know how to know themselves.

The most important task for those who study the art of screen performance is to fully and thoroughly know themselves. Except for the number of eyebrows and eyelashes that do not need to be counted clearly, we must examine every part of our face, which is a component of beauty and which is a component of ugliness, just like an accountant examining the assets of the person involved, with no omission. This is a necessary job for everyone who loves themselves, and is not limited to film actors.
